
* Learning
- [[http://www.freeminded.org/index.php/2012/04/hdparm-power-down-drives-when-not-in-use/][hdparm: power down drives when not in use @ Freeminded.org]]
- [[https://habr.com/ru/companies/ruvds/articles/736538/][Расследуем фантомные чтения с диска в Linux / Хабр]]

* Tools
- [[https://github.com/diskoverdata/diskover-community][diskoverdata/diskover-community: Diskover Community Edition - Open source file indexer, file search engine and data management and analytics powered by Elasticsearch]]
- [[https://github.com/shundhammer/qdirstat][shundhammer/qdirstat: QDirStat - Qt-based directory statistics (KDirStat without any KDE - from the original KDirStat author)]]
  - [[https://hub.docker.com/r/linuxserver/qdirstat][linuxserver/qdirstat - Docker Image | Docker Hub]]
- [[https://github.com/imsnif/diskonaut][imsnif/diskonaut: Terminal disk space navigator]]
- [[https://github.com/tchajed/rust-nbd][tchajed/rust-nbd: Network Block Device (NBD) server and client written in Rust]]
- =fatrace= makes use of the linux fanotify API (more details) available since
  linux kernel 2.6.37.
- btrace or blktrace (a wrapper of btrace) track kernel block I/O and can help you there.
- [[https://github.com/thesourcerer8/hddsuperclone][thesourcerer8/hddsuperclone: HDDSuperClone, HDDSuperTool]]
- [[https://github.com/adelolmo/hd-idle][adelolmo/hd-idle: Hard Disk Idle Spin-Down Utility]]
- [[https://www.linuxserver.io/blog/2018-10-29-new-hard-drive-rituals][New Hard Drive rituals | LinuxServer.io]]
- ledctl

* WD

- [[https://support.wdc.com/downloads.aspx?p=201&lang=en][Software and Firmware Downloads | WD Support]]
- [[https://documents.westerndigital.com/content/dam/doc-library/en_us/assets/public/western-digital/product/internal-drives/wd-purple-hdd/whitepaper-generic-benefit-for-hard-disk-drive.pdf][White Paper: Western Digital Trim Command - General Benefits for Hard Disk Drives - whitepaper-generic-benefit-for-hard-disk-drive.pdf]]
- [[https://documents.westerndigital.com/content/dam/doc-library/en_us/assets/public/western-digital/product/internal-drives/wd-purple-pro-hdd/product-brief-wd-purple-pro-sata-hdd.pdf][Product Brief: Western Digital WD Purple Pro Series - product-brief-wd-purple-pro-sata-hdd.pdf]]

#+begin_example
  root@guixsd ~ [env]# hdparm -M 128 /dev/sdb

  /dev/sdb:
   setting acoustic management to 128
  SG_IO: bad/missing sense data, sb[]:  70 00 05 00 00 00 00 0a 04 53 00 00 21 04 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00
   acoustic      = not supported
#+end_example

#+begin_example
  root@guixsd ~# guix shell hdparm -- hdparm -S 60 /dev/sdb

  /dev/sdb:
   setting standby to 60 (5 minutes)
#+end_example
